❯ so yes, game halting and/or player halting rules. when a block is claimed by a bot, the block's grey area turns to

  square, and its fill / background color is the color of the bot. the bahavior of the game is that is a simulator with 
   a loop like this: while (not done) { for each bot, allow them to move one space, then, check for game end } - in     
  particular, notice how the 'chaos' bot may have to call random repeatedly until it's exhausted it's ability to move,  
  but lawnmower much have much simpler and less cpu time to decide - regardless of how long it takes, each bot gets     
  called to "makeMove()" and they move themselves, returning true from makeMove() if they could move, and return false  
  from makemove if they cannot.

● Write(specification.md)                                                                                               
   
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Create file                                                                                                          
 specification.md                                                                                                       
╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
    1 # Specification: Jason's Game Of Life (aka Land Grab Simulator)                                                   
    2                                                                                                                 
    3 ---
    4
    5 ## Overview
    6
    7 A browser-based visual simulation inspired by Conway's Game Of Life. A grid
       of cells is populated by autonomous bots that move around and claim territ
      ory. Bots cannot enter territory claimed by other bots. The simulation runs
       until all bots are stuck and cannot move.
    8
    9 ---
   10
   11 ## Technology
   12
   13 - Vanilla JS, HTML, CSS — no frameworks, no build step
   14 - Rendered on an HTML5 `<canvas>` element
   15 - Single `index.html` entry point
   16
   17 ---
   18
   19 ## Grid
   20
   21 - 50 columns × 100 rows
   22 - Each cell is 10×10 pixels
   23 - Each cell has a 1px transparent border (gap showing canvas background — c
      reates grid lines)
   24 - Drawable interior per cell: 8×8 pixels (offset 1px from cell origin)
   25 - Unclaimed cell fill color: grey (`#555555`)
   26 - Canvas background color: dark, to make grid lines visible
   27 - Total canvas size: 500×1000 pixels
   28
   29 ---
   30
   31 ## UI Controls
   32
   33 ### Speed slider
   34
   35 - A range input below the grid labeled "Speed"
   36 - 7 discrete steps (min=0, max=6), default at step 2 (1 second)
   37 - Step-to-delay mapping:
   38
   39 | Step | Delay     | Display |
   40 |------|-----------|---------|
   41 | 0    | 5000ms    | 5s      |
   42 | 1    | 2000ms    | 2s      |
   43 | 2    | 1000ms    | 1s      |
   44 | 3    | 500ms     | 1/2s    |
   45 | 4    | 250ms     | 1/4s    |
   46 | 5    | 125ms     | 1/8s    |
   47 | 6    | 62ms      | 1/16s   |
   48
   49 - Changing the slider mid-game takes effect immediately (restarts the inter
      val at the new speed)
   50 - A text label next to the slider displays the current speed value
   51
   52 ### Run Again button
   53
   54 - Labeled "Run Again"
   55 - Resets and restarts the simulation from scratch: new random bot positions
      , fresh grid
   56 - Works at any time — mid-game or after game over
   57
   58 ---
   59
   60 ## File Structure
   61
   62 ```
   63 index.html
   64 css/
   65   style.css
   66 js/
   67   game.js           — grid, game loop, rendering engine
   68   bots/
   69     lawnmower.js    — Lawnmower bot class
   70     chaos.js        — Chaos bot class
   71 specification.md
   72 ```
   73
   74 New bots are added by creating a new file in `js/bots/` and adding a `<scri
      pt>` tag in `index.html` before `game.js`.
   75
   76 ---
   77
   78 ## Bot Interface
   79
   80 Every bot class must implement this interface:
   81
   82 ```
   83 constructor(game, col, row, color)
   84   game   — reference to the Game object (for canMoveTo / moveBotTo calls)
   85   col    — starting column (0-indexed)
   86   row    — starting row (0-indexed)
   87   color  — CSS color string
   88
   89 Properties (set by constructor, readable by Game):
   90   this.col    — current column
   91   this.row    — current row
   92   this.color  — bot's color string
   93   this.dead   — boolean, initialized to false
   94
   95 makeMove() → boolean
   96   Called once per game tick by the game loop.
   97   Must move the bot exactly one cell if possible.
   98   Returns true if the bot moved, false if it cannot move at all.
   99   When false is returned, the game loop marks the bot dead and never calls
      makeMove() again.
  100 ```
  101
  102 Bots call `game.canMoveTo(col, row, this)` to check a cell and `game.moveBo
      tTo(this, col, row)` to execute a move. Bots do not directly modify the cel
      ls array.
  103
  104 ---
  105
  106 ## Game API (available to bots)
  107
  108 ```
  109 game.canMoveTo(col, row, bot) → boolean
  110   Returns true if the cell at (col, row) is within bounds AND is either
  111   unclaimed (null) or claimed by this bot. Returns false otherwise.
  112
  113 game.moveBotTo(bot, col, row)
  114   Updates bot.col, bot.row, and marks cells[row][col] = bot.
  115   Does NOT clear the previous cell — territory is permanent.
  116 ```
  117
  118 ---
  119
  120 ## Cell Ownership
  121
  122 - `cells[row][col]` is `null` (unclaimed) or a bot reference (claimed by th
      at bot)
  123 - When a bot moves to a cell, that cell is permanently set to that bot (ter
      ritory is never lost)
  124 - A bot may re-enter cells it has previously claimed
  125 - A bot may not enter cells claimed by a different bot
  126
  127 ---
  128
  129 ## Bot Rendering
  130
  131 Bots are drawn on top of the cell layer each frame, at their current `col`/
      `row` position.
  132
  133 **Live bot:**
  134 - 8×8 white filled square at the cell's interior origin
  135 - 4×4 bot-color filled square centered inside (2px white border all around)
  136
  137 **Dead bot:**
  138 - 8×8 black filled square at the cell's interior origin
  139 - 4×4 bot-color filled square centered inside (2px black border all around)
  140 - Red X drawn corner-to-corner across the full 8×8 area, lineWidth 1.5
  141
  142 ---
  143
  144 ## Render Order (per frame)
  145
  146 1. Draw all cells (grey for unclaimed, bot color for claimed)
  147 2. Draw all bot markers on top
  148
  149 ---
  150
  151 ## Game Loop
  152
  153 ```
  154 setInterval(tick, currentSpeed)
  155
  156 tick():
  157   for each bot (in order):
  158     if not dead:
  159       result = bot.makeMove()
  160       if result is false:
  161         bot.dead = true
  162   render()
  163   if all bots are dead:
  164     stop the interval
  165 ```
  166
  167 The game does not automatically restart when over — the player clicks "Run
      Again."
  168
  169 ---
  170
  171 ## Bot: Lawnmower
  172
  173 **Name:** Lawnmower
  174 **Color:** Blue (`#4488ff`)
  175
  176 **Behavior:** Sweeps laterally (left/right) until blocked, then nudges one
      step vertically and reverses lateral direction. A classic lawnmower pattern
      .
  177
  178 **Initial state:**
  179 - Lateral direction: randomly left or right
  180
  181 **Each tick (makeMove):**
  182 1. Try to move one step in the current lateral direction
  183 2. If that cell is available → move there, return true
  184 3. If blocked → try to nudge vertically:
  185    - Pick a random vertical direction (up or down) to try first
  186    - If that cell is available → move there, reverse lateral direction, ret
      urn true
  187    - If that cell is also blocked → try the other vertical direction
  188    - If that cell is available → move there, reverse lateral direction, ret
      urn true
  189    - If both vertical directions are blocked → return false (bot dies)
  190
  191 **Judgment calls:**
  192 - Lateral direction reverses on any block (wall or enemy territory), not ju
      st walls
  193 - Vertical direction is chosen randomly each time a nudge is needed (not re
      membered)
  194 - A nudge and a lateral move are separate ticks — each call to makeMove() m
      oves exactly one cell
  195
  196 ---
  197
  198 ## Bot: Chaos
  199
  200 **Name:** Chaos
  201 **Color:** Green (`#44cc44`)
  202
  203 **Behavior:** Moves one step in a random direction each tick. If blocked, t
      ries another random direction until it finds one that works or exhausts all
       options.
  204
  205 **Each tick (makeMove):**
  206 1. Shuffle all four directions randomly (up, down, left, right)
  207 2. Try each in shuffled order
  208 3. First available direction → move there, return true
  209 4. If all four are blocked → return false (bot dies)
  210
  211 **Note:** Shuffling all four directions before trying is functionally equiv
      alent to the described "try random, retry if blocked" behavior, and avoids
      any possibility of infinite loops.
  212
  213 ---
  214
  215 ## Initial Bot Placement
  216
  217 - Each bot is placed at a random cell on the grid
  218 - No two bots may start on the same cell
  219 - The starting cell is immediately claimed by that bot (cells[row][col] = b
      ot)
  220
  221 ---
  222
  223 ## Game End
  224
  225 - The game ends when all bots have `dead === true`
  226 - No winner announcement or scoring in the initial implementation
  227 - The interval is cleared; the grid remains frozen in its final state
  228 - The player clicks "Run Again" to start over
  229
  230 ---
  231
  232 ## Edge Cases
  233
      /Users/jason/Documents/code/claude/land-grab-sim/js/bots)

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Create file
 js/game.js                                                                                                             
╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
    1 const COLS = 50;                                                                                                  
    2 const ROWS = 100;                                                                                               
    3 const CELL_SIZE = 10;
    4
    5 const SPEEDS = [5000, 2000, 1000, 500, 250, 125, 62];
    6 const SPEED_LABELS = ['5s', '2s', '1s', '1/2s', '1/4s', '1/8s', '1/16s'];
    7
    8 const BOT_DEFS = [
    9   { Class: LawnmowerBot, color: '#4488ff' },
   10   { Class: ChaosBot,     color: '#44cc44' },
   11 ];
   12
   13 class Game {
   14   constructor(canvas) {
   15           this.canvas = canvas;
   16           this.ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
   17           canvas.width = COLS * CELL_SIZE;
   18           canvas.height = ROWS * CELL_SIZE;
   19           this.cells = null;
   20           this.bots = [];
   21           this.interval = null;
   22           this.currentSpeed = SPEEDS[2];
   23   }
   24
   25   start() {
   26           if (this.interval) {
   27                   clearInterval(this.interval);
   28                   this.interval = null;
   29           }
   30
   31           this.cells = Array.from({ length: ROWS }, () => new Array(COLS).fill(null))
      ;
   32           this.bots = this.spawnBots();
   33           this.render();
   34           this.interval = setInterval(() => this.tick(), this.currentSpeed);
   35   }
   36
   37   spawnBots() {
   38           const used = new Set();
   39           return BOT_DEFS.map(({ Class, color }) => {
   40                   let col, row;
   41                   do {
   42                           col = Math.floor(Math.random() * COLS);
   43                           row = Math.floor(Math.random() * ROWS);
   44                   } while (used.has(`${col},${row}`));
   45                   used.add(`${col},${row}`);
   46                   const bot = new Class(this, col, row, color);
   47                   this.cells[row][col] = bot;
   48                   return bot;
   49           });
   50   }
   51
   52   tick() {
   53           for (const bot of this.bots) {
   54                   if (!bot.dead) {
   55                           if (!bot.makeMove()) {
   56                                   bot.dead = true;
   57                           }
   58                   }
   59           }
   60
   61           this.render();
   62
   63           if (this.bots.every(b => b.dead)) {
   64                   clearInterval(this.interval);
   65                   this.interval = null;
   66           }
   67   }
   68
   69   render() {
   70           const ctx = this.ctx;
   71
   72           for (let r = 0; r < ROWS; r++) {
   73                   for (let c = 0; c < COLS; c++) {
   74                           const x = c * CELL_SIZE + 1;
   75                           const y = r * CELL_SIZE + 1;
   76                           const bot = this.cells[r][c];
   77                           ctx.fillStyle = bot ? bot.color : '#555555';
   78                           ctx.fillRect(x, y, 8, 8);
   79                   }
   80           }
   81
   82           for (const bot of this.bots) {
   83                   this.drawBot(bot);
   84           }
   85   }
   86
   87   drawBot(bot) {
   88           const ctx = this.ctx;
   89           const x = bot.col * CELL_SIZE + 1;
   90           const y = bot.row * CELL_SIZE + 1;
   91
   92           if (bot.dead) {
   93                   ctx.fillStyle = '#000000';
   94                   ctx.fillRect(x, y, 8, 8);
   95                   ctx.fillStyle = bot.color;
   96                   ctx.fillRect(x + 2, y + 2, 4, 4);
   97                   ctx.strokeStyle = '#ff0000';
   98                   ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
   99                   ctx.beginPath();
  100                   ctx.moveTo(x + 1, y + 1);
  101                   ctx.lineTo(x + 7, y + 7);
  102                   ctx.moveTo(x + 7, y + 1);
  103                   ctx.lineTo(x + 1, y + 7);
  104                   ctx.stroke();
  105           } else {
  106                   ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
  107                   ctx.fillRect(x, y, 8, 8);
  108                   ctx.fillStyle = bot.color;
  109                   ctx.fillRect(x + 2, y + 2, 4, 4);
  110           }
  111   }
  112
  113   canMoveTo(col, row, bot) {
  114           if (col < 0 || col >= COLS || row < 0 || row >= ROWS) return false;
  115           const cell = this.cells[row][col];
  116           return cell === null || cell === bot;
  117   }
  118
  119   moveBotTo(bot, col, row) {
  120           bot.col = col;
  121           bot.row = row;
  122           this.cells[row][col] = bot;
  123   }
  124
  125   setSpeed(speedMs) {
  126           this.currentSpeed = speedMs;
  127           if (this.interval) {
      5                 this.row = row;
      6                 this.color = color;
      7                 this.dead = false;
      8                 this.lateralDir = Math.random() < 0.5 ? -1 : 1;
      9         }
     … +18 lines (ctrl+o to expand)

   9
  10    makeMove() {
  11            let bestCol = null;
  12            let bestRow = null;
  13            let bestDist = Infinity;
  14
  15            for (let r = 0; r < ROWS; r++) {
  16                    for (let c = 0; c < COLS; c++) {
  17                            if (this.game.cells[r][c] === null) {
  18                                    const dist = Math.abs(c - this.col) + Math.abs(r - this.row);
  19                                    if (dist < bestDist) {
  20                                            bestDist = dist;
  21                                            bestCol = c;
  22                                            bestRow = r;
  23                                    }
  24                            }
  25                    }
  26            }
  27
  28            if (bestCol === null) return false;
  29
  30            const dc = Math.sign(bestCol - this.col);

╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
   1 class BigBoyBot {
   2    constructor(game, col, row, color) {
   3            this.game = game;
   4            this.col = col;
   5            this.row = row;
   6            this.color = color;
   7            this.dead = false;
   8            this.size = 2;
   9            this.skipNext = false;
  10    }
  11
  12    getNewCells(dc, dr) {
  13            if (dc !== 0) {
  14                    const x = this.col + (dc > 0 ? 2 : -1);
  15                    return [[x, this.row], [x, this.row + 1]];
  16            } else {
  17                    const y = this.row + (dr > 0 ? 2 : -1);
  18                    return [[this.col, y], [this.col + 1, y]];
  19            }
  20    }
  21
  22    canMove(dc, dr) {
  23            return this.getNewCells(dc, dr).every(([c, r]) => this.game.canMoveTo(c, r, this));
  24    }
  25
  26    doMove(dc, dr) {
  27            const newCells = this.getNewCells(dc, dr);
  28            const claimedNew = newCells.some(([c, r]) => this.game.cells[r][c] === null);
  29            for (const [c, r] of newCells) {
  30                    this.game.cells[r][c] = this;
  31            }
  32            this.movesSinceNewLand = claimedNew ? 0 : this.movesSinceNewLand + 1;
  33            this.col += dc;
  34            this.row += dr;
  35    }
      122    moveBotTo(bot, col, row) {
      123 +    if (this.cells[row][col] === null) {                                                              
      124 +      bot.movesSinceNewLand = 0;                                                                      
      125 +    } else {                                                                                          
      126 +      bot.movesSinceNewLand++;                                                                        
      127 +    }                                                                                                 
      128      bot.col = col;
      129      bot.row = row;
      130      this.cells[row][col] = bot;

● Done. Quick rundown of how Hydra works:                                                                               
                                                                                                                        
  - Shuffles directions randomly each tick (Chaos-style)                                                                
  - If the first direction it tries is valid — moves, no spawn                                                          
  - If it hits at least one block before finding a valid direction — spawns one child at its current position, then     
  moves away                                                                                                            
  - If all four are blocked — dies, no spawn (prevents infinite chains)                                                 
                                                                                                                        
  The child is left at the parent's old cell with the territory transferred to it, so it has a foothold to explore from.
   Give it a run — at high speed it should spread pretty aggressively.

● Done. Hydra now moves exactly like Chaos, and when it dies it spawns two children at its last position. The children
  will do the same when they die. Note that if a Hydra gets completely hemmed in with no grey adjacent cells, its
  children will also be immediately stuck and spawn their own children — it'll chain until the stagnation counter kills
  them. Worth keeping an eye on at high speeds.

❯ the big boy outline looks wrong, and on new run again, game board should be completely redrawn including black        
  borders for squares                                                                                                   

● Both issues share a root cause: the render loop only repaints the 8×8 cell interiors, leaving the 1px gap pixels
  untouched. When Big Boy draws its 18×18 white rect, those gap pixels turn white and never get cleared — including on
  Run Again. Fix is to wipe the canvas at the start of every render.

  While I'm in render, let me also look at the Big Boy draw math to see if the outline is off.

  Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

● Done. Here's what changed:         

  - Speed system: The game ticks at a fixed interval; each bot now has ticksPerMove (regular bots = 20, Big Boy = 10).  
  moveCooldown increments each tick and the bot only moves when it hits its threshold. skipNext is gone from BigBoyBot.
  - Speed Boost powerup: 10 glowing cyan blocks scattered on the grid. When any bot walks onto one, their ticksPerMove  
  drops to 5. Big Boy collects them too in doMove.                                                                      
  - Powerup panel: horizontal strip below the grid, same dark style as the bot panel. Unchecking a powerup type removes
  it from the next run.

╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
   1 class JezzBallBot {                                                                                                
   2    constructor(game, col, row, color) {                                                                          
   3            this.game = game;
   4            this.col = col;
   5            this.row = row;
   6            this.color = color;
   7            this.dead = false;
   8            this.size = 1;
   9            this.isLeader = false;
  10            this.teammates = [];
  11            this.dc = 0;
  12            this.dr = 0;
  13            this.stuck = true;
  14    }
  15
  16    get partner() {
  17            return this.teammates[0] || null;
  18    }
  19
  20    onGroupReady() {
  21            this.chooseNewAxis();
  22    }
  23
  24    chooseNewAxis() {
  25            const axes = [
  26                    [[-1, 0], [1, 0]],
  27                    [[0, -1], [0, 1]],
  28                    [[-1,-1], [1, 1]],
  29                    [[-1, 1], [1,-1]],
  30            ];
  31            const pair = axes[Math.floor(Math.random() * axes.length)];
  32            if (Math.random() < 0.5) {
  33                    [this.dc, this.dr] = pair[0];
  34                    [this.partner.dc, this.partner.dr] = pair[1];
  35            } else {
  36                    [this.dc, this.dr] = pair[1];
  37                    [this.partner.dc, this.partner.dr] = pair[0];
  38            }
  39            this.stuck = false;
  40            this.partner.stuck = false;
      50  </html>

● Done. Here's how it works:                              
            
  - Two bots (coral #ff6644) spawn at the same cell. The first is the leader.                                           
  - onGroupReady() is called on the leader right after spawn — it calls chooseNewAxis() which picks one of 4 axis pairs 
  (left/right, up/down, diag-A, diag-B) and assigns one direction to each bot, then clears their stuck flag.            
  - Each tick, each bot walks one step in its assigned direction. When it hits a wall or another color, it sets stuck = 
  true.                                                                                                                 
  - The leader watches both this.stuck and this.partner.stuck. When both are stuck, it calls chooseNewAxis() again and  
  they're off in a new pair of directions.                                                                              
  - If one bot is stuck waiting for the other, it increments movesSinceNewLand — so they can't wait forever without     
  consequence.                                                                                                          
  - Speed powerup on either bot propagates to the other via the existing teammates sync.

╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
   1 ## Game Specification — Land Grab Simulator
   2
   3 ---
   4
   5 ### Grid
   6
   7 - **Size**: 100 columns × 50 rows
   8 - **Cell size**: 10×10 pixels (rendered as 8×8 with a 1px gap on each side)
   9 - **Background color**: #555555 (unclaimed / "grey")
  10
  11 ---
  12
  13 ### Game Flow
  14
  15 1. On start (or "Run Again"), the grid is cleared and all active bots are spawned at random positions.
  16 2. The game runs for **30 seconds** of wall-clock time, independent of the tick speed setting.
  17 3. The game also ends early if all bots are dead before the 30 seconds elapse.
  18 4. When the game ends, all bots are marked dead and the final board state is frozen.
  19
  20 ---
  21
  22 ### Tick System
  23
  24 - The game advances by a **tick** at a configurable interval (controlled by the speed slider).
  25 - Speed options range from 5000ms/tick (slowest) to 4ms/tick (fastest), with 11 preset steps.
  26 - Each bot has a `ticksPerMove` property. A bot only attempts a move when its internal `moveCooldown` counter re
     aches `ticksPerMove`. This allows bots to move at different effective rates independently of the global tick spe
     ed.
  27 - Default `ticksPerMove` values:
  28   - Most single-cell bots: 10
  29   - Big Boy: 20
  30   - Scout: 30
  31   - Speed Boost powerup overrides any bot's `ticksPerMove` to 5
  32
  33 ---
  34
  35 ### Bot Movement
  36
  37 - Each tick, each living bot's `moveCooldown` increments by 1. When it equals `ticksPerMove`, the bot attempts a
      move and `moveCooldown` resets to 0.
  38 - A bot **cannot** move to a cell owned by a different bot. It can move to unclaimed (null) cells or cells it al
     ready owns.
  39 - When a bot moves to a cell, that cell becomes owned by that bot and is drawn in the bot's color.
  40 - Ownership is never revoked — once a bot claims a cell, no other bot can take it.
  41
  42 ---
  43
  44 ### Death Conditions
  45
  46 A bot dies if either of the following is true after its move attempt:
  47
  48 1. **Cannot move**: `makeMove()` returns `false` (all valid moves are blocked).
  49 2. **Stagnation**: The bot has gone **100 consecutive moves** without claiming any new (previously unclaimed) ce
     ll. The counter resets to 0 each time a new grey cell is claimed.
  50
  51 When all bots are dead, the game ends immediately (even before the 30-second clock expires).
  52
  53 ---
  54
  55 ### Scoring
  56
  57 - Each grid cell owned by a bot counts as **1 point** for that bot's team.
  58 - Multi-cell bots (e.g., Big Boy's 2×2 footprint) accumulate 1 point per cell, so a full 2×2 block = 4 points.
  59 - Scores are grouped by bot type (all instances of the same type share a score).
  60 - Scores are displayed live during the game, sorted from highest to lowest. The leading score is highlighted.
  61
  62 ---
  63
  64 ### Powerups
  65
  66 - Powerups are placed on random unclaimed cells at the start of each game.
  67 - A bot collects a powerup by moving onto its cell.
  68 - Currently one powerup type:
  69   - **Speed Boost**: sets the collecting bot's `ticksPerMove` to 5 (faster movement). If the bot has teammates,
     all teammates receive the same speed boost. A visual indicator (▲) appears next to the bot's name in the panel.
  70 - Powerup count and enabled state are configurable per powerup via the Powerups panel.
  71
  72 ---
  73
  (left/right, up/down, diag-A, diag-B) and assigns one direction to each bot, then clears their stuck flag.
  - Each tick, each bot walks one step in its assigned direction. When it hits a wall or another color, it sets stuck =
  true.
  - The leader watches both this.stuck and this.partner.stuck. When both are stuck, it calls chooseNewAxis() again and
  they're off in a new pair of directions.
  - If one bot is stuck waiting for the other, it increments movesSinceNewLand — so they can't wait forever without
  consequence.
  - Speed powerup on either bot propagates to the other via the existing teammates sync.

╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
   1 ## Bot Specifications — Land Grab Simulator                                                                        
   2                                                                                                                  
   3 Each bot entry covers: behavior, movement rules, death/special conditions, a
     nd any unique mechanics.
   4
   5 ---
   6
   7 ### Airport Line
   8 **Color**: #4488ff (blue) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1
   9
  10 Moves laterally (left or right) in a chosen direction until blocked by a wal
     l or another bot's color. When blocked laterally, steps one cell vertically
     (up or down) and reverses lateral direction for the next lateral sweep.
  11
  12 **Vertical nudge logic**: prefers the vertical direction that leads to an un
     claimed (grey) cell. If both or neither direction has a grey neighbor, picks
      randomly.
  13
  14 Repeats: sweep → nudge → sweep → nudge. Dies if it cannot move laterally or
     vertically when blocked.
  15
  16 ---
  17
  18 ### Chaos
  19 **Color**: #ff8800 (orange) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1
  20
  21 Every move, shuffles the four cardinal directions (up, down, left, right) ra
     ndomly and takes the first one that is a valid move. No memory, no strategy.
      Dies only when completely surrounded.
  22
  23 ---
  24
  25 ### Lawnmower
  26 **Color**: #44cc44 (green) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1
  27
  28 Maintains a current direction index cycling clockwise through: up → right →
     down → left. Each move, tries to advance in the current direction. If the ne
     xt cell is already owned by this bot, steps in the **opposite** direction in
     stead (to avoid retracing). If neither works, rotates clockwise to the next
     direction and tries again. Cycles through all four directions before giving
     up.
  29
  30 ---
  31
  32 ### Genghis
  33 **Color**: #cc2222 (red) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1
  34
  35 Every move, performs a full scan of the entire grid to find the nearest uncl
     aimed (grey) cell by Manhattan distance. Moves one step toward it: prefers t
     he axis with greater separation first, then tries the other axis. If no uncl
     aimed cells remain, dies.
  36
  37 ---
  38
  39 ### Big Boy
  40 **Color**: #ffdd00 (yellow) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 20 | **Size**: 2×2
  41
  42 Occupies a 2×2 block of cells at all times. Each move attempts to shift the
     entire 2×2 footprint one step in a randomly chosen cardinal direction, claim
     ing four new cells and vacating the previous four. A move is only valid if a
     ll four destination cells are either unclaimed or owned by Big Boy.
  43
  44 Rendered as a single joined 18×18 block. Each of the four cells counts indiv
     idually toward scoring (4 points per position).
  45
  46 ---
  47
  48 ### Hydra
  49 **Color**: #aa44ff (purple) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1
  50
  51 Moves like Chaos — random direction each turn. When completely blocked (all
     four cardinal directions are unavailable), instead of dying normally, it **s
     pawns two new Hydra bots** at its current position and then dies. The spawne
     d children behave identically and can also split when blocked.
  52
  53 ---
  54
  55 ### Scout
  56 **Color**: #ff55cc (pink) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 30 | **Count**: 3 bots p
     er team | **Size**: 1×1
  57
  58 Spawns as a team of 3 bots at the same starting position. Each bot independe
     ntly picks a random cardinal direction and moves in a straight line until bl
     ocked by a wall or a different color. When blocked, shuffles the remaining t
     hree directions and picks the first valid one.
  59
  60 Scouts treat cells owned by their own team (same color) as passable — they d
     o not stop when entering teammate territory, though this does not count as c
     laiming new land for stagnation purposes.
  61
  62 All three bots' cell counts are pooled into a single "Scout" score. If any s
     cout collects the Speed Boost powerup, all three teammates receive the speed
      boost simultaneously.
  63
  64 ---
  65
  66 ### Bishop
  67 **Color**: #00ccbb (teal) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1
  68
  69 Moves exclusively diagonally (never laterally or vertically). Picks a random
      diagonal direction at spawn — one of: up-left, up-right, down-left, down-ri
     ght — and keeps moving in that direction until blocked by a wall or another
     bot's color. When blocked, shuffles the other three diagonal directions and
     takes the first valid one. Dies if all four diagonals are blocked.
  70
  71 Due to diagonal-only movement, Bishop can only ever reach cells where `(col
     + row) % 2` matches its starting cell's parity — it covers at most half the
     grid.
  72
  73 ---
  74
  75 ### Jezzball
  76 **Color**: #ff6644 (coral) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Count**: 2 bots
     per team | **Size**: 1×1
  77
  78 Spawns as a pair at the same starting position. One bot is designated the **
  in that file

● Done. Here's how it works:

  - When a bot touches the Multiball powerup, one new bot of the same class spawns at that exact cell
  - The new bot inherits the collector's current ticksPerMove (so if the team already has a Speed Boost, the newcomer is
   already fast)
  - The new bot is added to the teammates array of every existing team member, and gets all of them as its own teammates
   — so a future Speed Boost or another Multiball will propagate to it too
  - Applies to any bot type: a solo bot like Chaos gets a teammate, Scout gains a 4th scout, Drunk Jezzball gains a 3rd
  pair member
  - The powerup count slider controls how many of each type appear, so you can tune the ratio in the New Game modal

  - New Game → starts immediately with whatever settings were last saved via OK                                         
  - Settings → opens the modal; snapshots current state so Cancel can fully revert any checkbox/slider changes made
  while browsing settings

 misc/game-spec.md                                                                                                      
╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
    4                                                                                                                   
    5  ### Grid                                                                                                         
    6                                                                                                                   
    7 -- **Size**: 100 columns × 50 rows                                                                               
    8 -- **Cell size**: 10×10 pixels (rendered as 8×8 with a 1px gap on each side)                                     
    9 -- **Background color**: #555555 (unclaimed / "grey")                                                            
    7 +- **Dimensions**: 100 columns × 50 rows (5,000 cells total)                                                     
    8 +- **Canvas size**: 1000×500 pixels (`COLS * CELL_SIZE` × `ROWS * CELL_SIZE`)                                    
    9 +- **Cell size**: 10×10 pixels per cell, rendered as an 8×8 filled square with a 1px transparent gap on the right
      + and bottom edge (so cells are visually separated)                                                              
   10 +- **Unclaimed cell color**: `#555555` (dark grey)                                                               
   11 +- **Background**: `#222222` canvas background, visible only through gaps                                        
   12  
   13  ---
   14  
   15  ### Game Flow
   16  
   15 -1. On start (or "Run Again"), the grid is cleared and all active bots are spawned at random positions.          
   16 -2. The game runs for **30 seconds** of wall-clock time, independent of the tick speed setting.                  
   17 -3. The game also ends early if all bots are dead before the 30 seconds elapse.                                  
   18 -4. When the game ends, all bots are marked dead and the final board state is frozen.                            
   17 +1. A game starts automatically on page load.                                                                    
   18 +2. Clicking **New Game** immediately restarts with the current saved settings — no confirmation.                
   19 +3. Clicking **Settings** opens a modal where bot/powerup/game-length options can be configured. **OK** saves and
      + closes; **Cancel** fully reverts any changes made while the modal was open (checkboxes and sliders are restored
      + to their pre-open state). The game keeps running behind the modal.                                             
   20 +4. On start, all timers and intervals from the previous game are cleared, the grid is wiped, bots are spawned, p
      +owerups are placed, and the clock begins.                                                                       
   21 +5. The game ends when **either** of the following occurs:                                                       
   22 +   - The game-length timer expires (see Clock section).                                                         
   23 +   - All bots are simultaneously dead.                                                                          
   24 +6. When the game ends, all bots are marked dead, all intervals are cleared, and the board freezes at its final s
      +tate.                                                                                                           
   25  
   26  ---
   27  
   28  ### Tick System
   29  
   24 -- The game advances by a **tick** at a configurable interval (controlled by the speed slider).                  
   25 -- Speed options range from 5000ms/tick (slowest) to 4ms/tick (fastest), with 11 preset steps.                   
   26 -- Each bot has a `ticksPerMove` property. A bot only attempts a move when its internal `moveCooldown` counter re
      -aches `ticksPerMove`. This allows bots to move at different effective rates independently of the global tick spe
      -ed.                                                                                                             
   27 -- Default `ticksPerMove` values:                                                                                
   28 -  - Most single-cell bots: 10                                                                                   
   29 -  - Big Boy: 20                                                                                                 
   30 -  - Scout: 30                                                                                                   
   31 -  - Speed Boost powerup overrides any bot's `ticksPerMove` to 5                                                 
   30 +The core loop runs via `setInterval` at the **tick interval** — the global speed set by the speed slider. Every 
      +tick:                                                                                                           
   31 +1. Each living bot's `moveCooldown` counter increments by 1.                                                    
   32 +2. When `moveCooldown >= ticksPerMove`, the bot attempts a move and `moveCooldown` resets to 0.                 
   33 +3. `render()` is called (redraws canvas + updates score panel).                                                 
   34 +4. If all bots are dead, the game stops.                                                                        
   35  
   36 +**Speed slider** (11 steps, adjustable while a game is running):                                                
   37 +                                                                                                                
   38 +| Index | Tick interval | Label  |                                                                              
   39 +|-------|--------------|--------|                                                                               
   40 +| 0     | 5000ms       | 5s     |                                                                               
   41 +| 1     | 2000ms       | 2s     |                                                                               
   42 +| 2     | 1000ms       | 1s     |                                                                               
   43 +| 3     | 500ms        | 1/2s   |                                                                               
   44 +| 4     | 250ms        | 1/4s   |                                                                               
   45 +| 5     | 125ms        | 1/8s   |                                                                               
   46 +| 6     | 62ms         | 1/16s  |                                                                               
   47 +| 7     | 31ms         | 1/32s  |                                                                               
   48 +| 8     | 16ms         | 1/64s  |                                                                               
   49 +| 9     | 8ms          | 1/128s |                                                                               
   50 +| 10    | 4ms          | 1/256s |                                                                               
   51 +                                                                                                                
   52 +Default speed on page load: index 9 (8ms/tick). Changing speed via the slider takes effect immediately mid-game.
   53 +                                                                                                                
   54 +**`ticksPerMove` values by bot type** (default, before powerups):                                               
   55 +                                                                                                                
   56 +| Bot              | ticksPerMove |                                                                             
   57 +|------------------|-------------|                                                                              
   58 +| Airport Line     | 10          |                                                                              
   59 +| Chaos            | 10          |                                                                              
   60 +| Lawnmower        | 10          |                                                                              
   61 +| Genghis          | 10          |                                                                              
   62 +| Big Boy          | 20          |                                                                              
   63 +| Hydra            | 10          |                                                                              
   64 +| Scout            | 30          |                                                                              
   65 +| Bishop           | 10          |                                                                              
   66 +| Drunk Jezzball   | 20          |                                                                              
   67 +                                                                                                                
   68  ---
   69  
   35 -### Bot Movement                                                                                                
   70 +### Bot Movement and Cell Ownership                                                                             
   71  
   37 -- Each tick, each living bot's `moveCooldown` increments by 1. When it equals `ticksPerMove`, the bot attempts a
      - move and `moveCooldown` resets to 0.                                                                           
   38 -- A bot **cannot** move to a cell owned by a different bot. It can move to unclaimed (null) cells or cells it al
      -ready owns.                                                                                                     
   39 -- When a bot moves to a cell, that cell becomes owned by that bot and is drawn in the bot's color.              
   40 -- Ownership is never revoked — once a bot claims a cell, no other bot can take it.                              
   72 +- A bot can move to a cell if it is **null** (unclaimed) or already owned by that exact bot instance.           
   73 +- A bot **cannot** move to a cell owned by any other bot instance, including teammates (except Scout, which has 
      +custom same-color passthrough logic).                                                                           
   74 +- When a bot moves to a cell via `moveBotTo()`, that cell's ownership is set to the bot and is never revoked by 
      +any other game mechanic (no ownership stealing).                                                                
   75 +- Big Boy moves its entire 2×2 footprint as a unit; all four destination cells must be available.               
   76  
   77  ---
   78  
   44 -### Death Conditions                                                                                            
   79 +### Death Condition                                                                                             
   80  
   46 -A bot dies if either of the following is true after its move attempt:                                           
   81 +A bot dies if `makeMove()` returns `false` — meaning it could find no valid move in any direction it tried. Ther
      +e is **no stagnation death** — bots that are temporarily stuck but not completely surrounded can keep trying ind
      +efinitely.                                                                                                      
   82  
   48 -1. **Cannot move**: `makeMove()` returns `false` (all valid moves are blocked).                                 
   49 -2. **Stagnation**: The bot has gone **100 consecutive moves** without claiming any new (previously unclaimed) ce
      -ll. The counter resets to 0 each time a new grey cell is claimed.                                               
   83 +When all bots are dead the game ends (timers stop, board freezes).                                              
   84  
   51 -When all bots are dead, the game ends immediately (even before the 30-second clock expires).                    
   85 +---                                                                                                             
   86  
   87 +### Spawning                                                                                                    
   88 +                                                                                                                
   89 +On game start, `spawnBots()` processes each enabled bot definition:                                             
   90 +1. A random starting position `(col, row)` is chosen, avoiding overlap with already-used cells (tracked in a `us
      +ed` set).                                                                                                       
   91 +2. For multi-bot teams (`count > 1`), `count` bot instances are created at the **same** starting position.      
   92 +3. All bots in a group get a `teammates` array containing every other member of the group.                      
   93 +4. The first bot in the group gets `isLeader = true`. If the bot class defines `onGroupReady()`, it is called on
      + the leader immediately after the group is linked (used by Drunk Jezzball to pick an initial axis).             
   94 +5. The starting cell(s) are assigned to the last bot in the group.                                              
   95 +6. Each spawned bot gets: `defIndex` (index into `BOT_DEFS`), `movesSinceNewLand = 0`, `ticksPerMove` from its d
      +ef, `moveCooldown = 0`.                                                                                         
   96 +                                                                                                                
   97 +Mid-game spawns (Hydra children, Multiball) use `spawnMidGame()` or direct construction and push to `game.bots` 
      +without the position-finding logic.                                                                             
   98 +                                                                                                                
   99  ---
  100  
  101  ### Scoring
  102  
   57 -- Each grid cell owned by a bot counts as **1 point** for that bot's team.                                      
   58 -- Multi-cell bots (e.g., Big Boy's 2×2 footprint) accumulate 1 point per cell, so a full 2×2 block = 4 points.  
   59 -- Scores are grouped by bot type (all instances of the same type share a score).                                
   60 -- Scores are displayed live during the game, sorted from highest to lowest. The leading score is highlighted.   
  103 +- Each cell in the grid owned by a bot contributes **1 point** to that bot's type's score.                      
  104 +- Scores are grouped by `defIndex` — all instances of the same bot type (including Hydra children, Scout teammat
      +es, Multiball spawns) share a combined score.                                                                   
  105 +- Big Boy's 2×2 footprint occupies 4 cells → 4 points.                                                          
  106 +- Scores are recalculated every render frame by scanning all 5,000 cells.                                       
  107 +- The score panel shows all types with at least one owned cell, sorted highest to lowest. The type(s) tied for t
      +he highest score are highlighted (name white, score yellow).                                                    
  108  
  109  ---
  110  
  111  ### Powerups
  112  
   66 -- Powerups are placed on random unclaimed cells at the start of each game.                                      
   67 -- A bot collects a powerup by moving onto its cell.                                                             
   68 -- Currently two powerup types:                                                                                  
   69 -  - **Speed Boost**: sets the collecting bot's `ticksPerMove` to 5 (faster movement). If the bot has teammates, 
      -all teammates receive the same speed boost. A visual indicator (▲) appears next to the bot's name in the panel. 
   70 -  - **Multiball**: spawns one new bot of the same type at the collecting bot's current position. The new bot inh
      -erits the collector's current speed and joins its teammates network. Only one new bot is spawned regardless of t
      -eam size.                                                                                                       
   71 -- Powerup count and enabled state are configurable per powerup via the Powerups panel.                          
  113 +Powerups are placed on random null cells at game start. The **count** slider (1–10, default 3) controls the tota
      +l number of powerups placed across all enabled types. Each powerup slot is assigned a random type from the enabl
      +ed types — so if both Speed Boost and Multiball are enabled and count is 6, the split is random (e.g., 4 speed +
      + 2 multiball).                                                                                                  
  114  
  115 +A bot collects a powerup the moment it moves onto the powerup's cell (`moveBotTo` calls `collectPowerup`). The p
      +owerup's `apply(bot)` function fires immediately and the powerup is removed from the board.                     
  116 +                                                                                                                
  117 +All powerups look **identical** on the grid — a rainbow-cycling 8×8 CSS-animated block — so bots cannot predict 
      +what they'll get. (Mystery box design.)                                                                         
  118 +                                                                                                                
  119 +**Powerup types:**                                                                                              
  120 +                                                                                                                
  121 +#### Speed Boost                                                                                                
  122 +- Sets the collecting bot's `ticksPerMove` to **5** (roughly 2–4× faster than most bots).                       
  123 +- If the bot has a `teammates` array, all teammates also get `ticksPerMove = 5`.                                
  124 +- A ▲ indicator appears next to the bot type's name in the side panel. Cleared on next game start.              
  125 +                                                                                                                
  126 +#### Multiball                                                                                                  
  127 +- Spawns **one** new bot of the same type at the collecting bot's current cell.                                 
  128 +- The new bot inherits the collector's current `ticksPerMove` (so if the team already has a Speed Boost, the new
      + member starts fast).                                                                                           
  129 +- The new bot is added to every existing team member's `teammates` array, and receives all of them as its own te
      +ammates.                                                                                                        
  130 +- Only one bot is spawned regardless of how many teammates already exist.                                       
  131 +- The new bot is pushed to `game.bots` and begins acting immediately next tick.                                 
  132 +                                                                                                                
  133 +#### instant death!!!                                                                                           
  134 +- Sets `bot.dead = true` on the collecting bot.                                                                 
  135 +- Sets `dead = true` on every bot in `bot.teammates`.                                                           
  136 +- The entire team dies simultaneously on the tick the powerup is collected.                                     
  137 +                                                                                                                
  138  ---
  139  
  140 +### Clock and Game Length                                                                                       
  141 +                                                                                                                
  142 +The clock runs on a 50ms `setInterval`, independent of the game tick speed. It is wall-clock time, not tick-coun
      +t.                                                                                                              
  143 +                                                                                                                
  144 +**Game length options** (set in Settings modal):                                                                
  145 +                                                                                                                
  146 +| Slider index | Duration  | Label |                                                                            
  147 +|-------------|-----------|-------|                                                                             
  148 +| 0           | 30 seconds | 30s  |                                                                             
  149 +| 1           | 1 minute   | 1m   |                                                                             
  150 +| 2           | 2 minutes  | 2m   |                                                                             
  151 +| 3           | 5 minutes  | 5m   |                                                                             
  152 +| 4           | No limit   | ∞    |                                                                             
  153 +                                                                                                                
  154 +Default: 30 seconds.                                                                                            
  155 +                                                                                                                
  156 +**Clock display behavior:**                                                                                     
  157 +- `remaining > 10s`: shows whole seconds (e.g., `23s`), normal grey color.                                      
  158 +- `remaining ≤ 10s`: shows seconds + two decimal places (e.g., `9.45s`), turns red, flashes via CSS animation.  
  159 +- `remaining = 0` (timer expired): calls `endGame()`, display changes to `game over` in static red, no flash.   
  160 +- `duration = ∞`: displays `∞`, no countdown, no timeout is set, game runs until all bots are dead.             
  161 +                                                                                                                
  162 +---                                                                                                             
  163 +                                                                                                                
  164  ### Rendering
  165  
   77 -- The grid is drawn on an HTML5 Canvas element every tick.                                                      
   78 -- The canvas is cleared fully each frame to prevent artifacts.                                                  
   79 -- Bot position markers are drawn as white-bordered squares with a colored interior. Dead bots show a red X.     
   80 -- A separate DOM overlay (`#powerup-overlay`) renders CSS-animated powerup blocks above the canvas using absolut
      -e positioning.                                                                                                  
   81 -- Big Boy's 2×2 territory is rendered as a single joined block when all four cells are confirmed to belong to th
      -e same bot instance.                                                                                            
  166 +Every render frame:                                                                                             
  167 +1. `ctx.clearRect()` wipes the entire canvas.                                                                   
  168 +2. All 5,000 cells are scanned. Each cell is drawn as an 8×8 filled rect at `(col*10+1, row*10+1)` in the owning
      + bot's color, or `#555555` if unclaimed.                                                                        
  169 +3. **Big Boy special case**: when scanning, if a 2×2 block of cells all belong to the same bot instance with `si
      +ze === 2`, a single 18×18 rect is drawn (spanning both cells minus the gap) and those four positions are marked 
      +visited to avoid redundant drawing.                                                                             
  170 +4. Each bot's current position is drawn as a **marker**: a white-bordered square (full cell size minus 2px) with
      + a colored inner square (inset 2px on each side).                                                               
  171 +   - **Alive**: white border, bot-color fill.                                                                   
  172 +   - **Dead**: black border, bot-color fill, red X (two diagonal lines across the cell).                        
  173 +5. `updateScores()` is called to refresh the score panel DOM.                                                   
  174 +6. A DOM overlay (`#powerup-overlay`) sits above the canvas with `pointer-events: none` and contains one `<div c
      +lass="powerup-block">` per active powerup, positioned with absolute `left`/`top` to align with the grid. Each bl
      +ock runs a `@keyframes rainbow-glow` CSS animation cycling through red → orange → yellow → green → blue → violet
      +. Collected powerups have their DOM element removed immediately.                                                
  175  
  176  ---
  177  
   85 -### UI Panels                                                                                                   
  178 +### UI Layout                                                                                                   
  179  
   87 -- **Bot panel** (right side): one checkbox per bot type. Only checked bots spawn on the next run. Shows a ▲ indi
      -cator when a bot holds the Speed Boost.                                                                         
   88 -- **Score panel** (below bot list): live score per bot type, sorted by score, leader highlighted.               
   89 -- **Clock** (below scores): counts down from 30s. Above 10s shows whole seconds. At 10s and below, switches to s
      -econds+milliseconds format, turns red, and flashes.                                                             
   90 -- **Powerup panel** (bottom): one checkbox per powerup type to enable/disable it for the next run.              
   91 -- **Speed slider**: controls global tick interval. Changes take effect immediately.                             
   92 -- **Run Again button**: resets and restarts the simulation with the current bot/powerup selection.              
  180 +```                                                                                                             
  181 +[Title]                                                                                                         
  182 +                                                                                                                
       91 -- **Speed slider**: controls global tick interval. Changes take effect immediately.                         
       92 -- **Run Again button**: resets and restarts the simulation with the current bot/powerup selection.

    1  ## Bot Specifications — Land Grab Simulator
    2  
    3 -Each bot entry covers: behavior, movement rules, death/special conditions, and any unique mechanics.            
    3 +Each entry covers: identity, movement algorithm (step by step), death condition, powerup interactions, and edge 
      +cases.

    5  ---
    6  
    7  ### Airport Line
    8 -**Color**: #4488ff (blue) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1                                          
    8  
   10 -Moves laterally (left or right) in a chosen direction until blocked by a wall or another bot's color. When block
      -ed laterally, steps one cell vertically (up or down) and reverses lateral direction for the next lateral sweep. 
    9 +**Class**: `AirportLineBot` | **File**: `js/bots/airport-line.js`                                               
   10 +**Color**: `#4488ff` (blue) | **ticksPerMove**: 10 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 1                      
   11  
   12 -**Vertical nudge logic**: prefers the vertical direction that leads to an unclaimed (grey) cell. If both or neit
      -her direction has a grey neighbor, picks randomly.                                                              
   12 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
   13  
   14 -Repeats: sweep → nudge → sweep → nudge. Dies if it cannot move laterally or vertically when blocked.            
   14 +Simulates a airport terminal moving walkway: sweeps left or right continuously, stepping vertically when it hits
      + a wall or another bot.                                                                                         
   15  
   16 +#### State                                                                                                      
   17 +                                                                                                                
   18 +| Property | Set at | Purpose |                                                                                 
   19 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
   20 +| `lateralDir` | Constructor | `+1` (right) or `-1` (left), chosen randomly at spawn |                          
   21 +                                                                                                                
   22 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
   23 +                                                                                                                
   24 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
   25 +                                                                                                                
   26 +1. **Attempt a lateral move** in the current `lateralDir` (i.e., `[this.col + lateralDir, this.row]`).          
   27 +   - If that cell passes `canMoveTo`: move there, return `true`. No state change.                               
   28 +2. **Lateral is blocked** — attempt a vertical nudge to the cell directly above or below (same column):         
   29 +   - Inspect the cells at `[this.col, this.row - 1]` (up) and `[this.col, this.row + 1]` (down).                
   30 +   - Classify each as "grey" (unclaimed, `=== null`) or not.                                                    
   31 +   - **Direction preference**:                                                                                  
   32 +     - Up-grey only → try `[-1, +1]` (up first, then down as fallback).                                         
   33 +     - Down-grey only → try `[+1, -1]` (down first, then up as fallback).                                       
   34 +     - Both grey or neither grey → randomly choose which to try first (50/50).                                  
   35 +   - For each candidate vertical direction in the ordered list: if `canMoveTo` passes, move there, **reverse `la
      +teralDir`**, return `true`.                                                                                     
   36 +3. If no lateral and no vertical move succeeded: return `false` → **bot dies**.                                 
   37 +                                                                                                                
   38 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
   39 +                                                                                                                
   40 +Dies only when the lateral cell is blocked AND both vertical neighbors are also blocked.                        
   41 +                                                                                                                
   42 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
   43 +                                                                                                                
   44 +- **Speed Boost**: `ticksPerMove` drops to 5 — sweeps faster.                                                   
   45 +- **Multiball**: spawns a second Airport Line at current position; it picks its own random `lateralDir` independ
      +ently.                                                                                                          
   46 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills this bot (and any teammates if multiball-spawned).                                
   47 +                                                                                                                
   48 +#### Edge Cases                                                                                                 
   49 +                                                                                                                
   50 +- Vertical nudge checks for "grey" using a raw `=== null` test on the cell value, **not** `canMoveTo`. A cell ow
      +ned by any bot (even this one) is not grey. This means the preference logic can favor a direction that is actual
      +ly blocked; the fallback direction is tried if so.                                                              
   51 +- A bot reaching a corner may find both its lateral and its nudge directions blocked simultaneously, resulting i
      +n death.                                                                                                        
   52 +

   55  ### Chaos
   19 -**Color**: #ff8800 (orange) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1                                        
   56  
   21 -Every move, shuffles the four cardinal directions (up, down, left, right) randomly and takes the first one that 
      -is a valid move. No memory, no strategy. Dies only when completely surrounded.                                  
   57 +**Class**: `ChaosBot` | **File**: `js/bots/chaos.js`                                                            
   58 +**Color**: `#ff8800` (orange) | **ticksPerMove**: 10 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 1                    
   59  
   60 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
   61 +                                                                                                                
   62 +Purely random. No memory, no strategy. Wanders until trapped.                                                   
   63 +                                                                                                                
   64 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
   65 +                                                                                                                
   66 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
   67 +                                                                                                                
   68 +1. Start with direction array `[[0,-1],[0,1],[-1,0],[1,0]]` (up, down, left, right).                            
   69 +2. Fisher-Yates shuffle the array in-place.                                                                     
   70 +3. Iterate through the shuffled directions; take the first one where `canMoveTo` returns `true`. Return `true`. 
   71 +4. If no direction is valid: return `false` → **bot dies**.                                                     
   72 +                                                                                                                
   73 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
   74 +                                                                                                                
   75 +Dies only when all four cardinal neighbors are blocked (wall or any other bot's color).                         
   76 +                                                                                                                
   77 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
   78 +                                                                                                                
   79 +- **Speed Boost**: `ticksPerMove` drops to 5.                                                                   
   80 +- **Multiball**: spawns another Chaos bot; the new one also shuffles independently.                             
   81 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills this bot immediately.                                                             
   82 +
