   85  ### Lawnmower
   26 -**Color**: #44cc44 (green) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1                                         
   86  
   28 -Maintains a current direction index cycling clockwise through: up → right → down → left. Each move, tries to adv
      -ance in the current direction. If the next cell is already owned by this bot, steps in the **opposite** directio
      -n instead (to avoid retracing). If neither works, rotates clockwise to the next direction and tries again. Cycle
      -s through all four directions before giving up.                                                                 
   87 +**Class**: `LawnmowerBot` | **File**: `js/bots/lawnmower.js`                                                    
   88 +**Color**: `#44cc44` (green) | **ticksPerMove**: 10 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 1                     
   89  
   90 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
   91 +                                                                                                                
   92 +Travels in a persistent direction, avoiding already-claimed cells by reversing; rotates clockwise when stuck.   
   93 +                                                                                                                
   94 +#### State                                                                                                      
   95 +                                                                                                                
   96 +| Property | Set at | Purpose |                                                                                 
   97 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
   98 +| `dirIndex` | Constructor | Index into the direction array, initialized randomly (0–3) |                       
   99 +                                                                                                                
  100 +Direction array (fixed order):                                                                                  
  101 +                                                                                                                
  102 +| Index | Direction | `[dc, dr]` |                                                                              
  103 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
  104 +| 0 | Up | `[0, -1]` |                                                                                          
  105 +| 1 | Right | `[1, 0]` |                                                                                        
  106 +| 2 | Down | `[0, 1]` |                                                                                         
  107 +| 3 | Left | `[-1, 0]` |                                                                                        
  108 +                                                                                                                
  109 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  110 +                                                                                                                
  111 +Each tick, up to 4 attempts (one per direction):                                                                
  112 +                                                                                                                
  113 +1. Read `[dc, dr]` from `dirs[dirIndex]`.                                                                       
  114 +2. Compute `nextCol = this.col + dc`, `nextRow = this.row + dr`.                                                
  115 +3. **If `canMoveTo(nextCol, nextRow)` is true**:                                                                
  116 +   - **If the target cell is already owned by this bot** (`isOwnCell` check):                                   
  117 +     - Compute opposite direction index: `(dirIndex + 2) % 4`.                                                  
  118 +     - If `canMoveTo` in the opposite direction passes: set `dirIndex` to opposite, move there, return `true`.  
  119 +     - Otherwise: fall through to rotation (do not move).                                                       
  120 +   - **If the target cell is not owned by this bot** (null or out-of-bounds-but-valid):                         
  121 +     - Move there, return `true`.                                                                               
  122 +4. **If `canMoveTo` is false or we fell through**: rotate clockwise — `dirIndex = (dirIndex + 1) % 4`.          
  123 +5. After 4 rotations with no successful move: return `false` → **bot dies**.                                    
  124 +                                                                                                                
  125 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  126 +                                                                                                                
  127 +Dies when all four cardinal directions are either blocked (wall, other bot) or owned by itself (and their opposi
      +tes are also blocked).                                                                                          
  128 +                                                                                                                
  129 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
  130 +                                                                                                                
  131 +- **Speed Boost**: `ticksPerMove` drops to 5; the bot sweeps the grid faster.                                   
  132 +- **Multiball**: spawns a second Lawnmower at current position with its own random `dirIndex`.                  
  133 +                                                                                                                
  134  ---
  135  
  136  ### Genghis
   33 -**Color**: #cc2222 (red) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1                                           
  137  
   35 -Every move, performs a full scan of the entire grid to find the nearest unclaimed (grey) cell by Manhattan dista
      -nce. Moves one step toward it: prefers the axis with greater separation first, then tries the other axis. If no 
      -unclaimed cells remain, dies.                                                                                   
  138 +**Class**: `GenghisBot` | **File**: `js/bots/genghis.js`                                                        
  139 +**Color**: `#cc2222` (red) | **ticksPerMove**: 10 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 1                       
  140  
  141 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
  142 +                                                                                                                
  143 +Hunts the nearest unclaimed cell on every tick using a full grid scan and Manhattan distance.                   
  144 +                                                                                                                
  145 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  146 +                                                                                                                
  147 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
  148 +                                                                                                                
  149 +1. **Grid scan**: iterate all 5,000 cells (`r` from 0 to ROWS-1, `c` from 0 to COLS-1). Track the cell `(bestCol
      +, bestRow)` with the smallest Manhattan distance `|c - this.col| + |r - this.row|` where `cells[r][c] === null`.
  150 +2. **If no null cell found**: return `false` → **bot dies** (the entire grid is claimed).                       
  151 +3. Compute `dc = Math.sign(bestCol - this.col)`, `dr = Math.sign(bestRow - this.row)`. Each is `-1`, `0`, or `+1
      +`.                                                                                                              
  152 +4. **Build move priority list**:                                                                                
  153 +   - If `dc !== 0`: add `[dc, 0]` (column-axis step toward target).                                             
  154 +   - If `dr !== 0`: add `[0, dr]` (row-axis step toward target).                                                
  155 +   - If both `dc !== 0` and `dr !== 0`: also add `[0, dr]` and `[dc, 0]` again (effectively ensuring both forwar
      +d directions appear).                                                                                           
  156 +   - Always append `[-dc, 0]` and `[0, -dr]` as last-resort backward moves.                                     
  157 +5. Skip any `[0, 0]` entries (can occur if dc or dr is 0 and we appended their negatives).                      
  158 +6. Try each move in order: first passing `canMoveTo` wins — move there, return `true`.                          
  159 +7. If none pass: return `false` → **bot dies**.                                                                 
  160 +                                                                                                                
  161 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  162 +                                                                                                                
  163 +Dies when unclaimed cells still exist but every cardinal neighbor is blocked, OR when the entire grid is claimed
      +.                                                                                                               
  164 +                                                                                                                
  165 +#### Notes                                                                                                      
  166 +                                                                                                                
  167 +- The scan order (row-major, top-to-bottom, left-to-right) means ties in Manhattan distance resolve to the topmo
      +st-leftmost unclaimed cell.                                                                                     
  168 +- Move priority always puts the column-axis step before the row-axis step (not the axis with greater separation)
      +. Both forward directions are tried, then backward directions.                                                  
  169 +                                                                                                                
  170  ---
  171  
  172  ### Big Boy
   40 -**Color**: #ffdd00 (yellow) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 20 | **Size**: 2×2                                        
  173  
   42 -Occupies a 2×2 block of cells at all times. Each move attempts to shift the entire 2×2 footprint one step in a r
      -andomly chosen cardinal direction, claiming four new cells and vacating the previous four. A move is only valid 
      -if all four destination cells are either unclaimed or owned by Big Boy.                                         
  174 +**Class**: `BigBoyBot` | **File**: `js/bots/big-boy.js`                                                         
  175 +**Color**: `#ffdd00` (yellow) | **ticksPerMove**: 20 | **Size**: 2×2 | **Count per team**: 1                    
  176  
   44 -Rendered as a single joined 18×18 block. Each of the four cells counts individually toward scoring (4 points per
      - position).                                                                                                     
  177 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
  178  
  179 +Occupies and claims a 2×2 block of cells. Each move, the entire footprint jumps 2 cells in a randomly chosen car
      +dinal direction, claiming 4 new cells. Old cells remain claimed permanently.                                    
  180 +                                                                                                                
  181 +#### State                                                                                                      
  182 +                                                                                                                
  183 +| Property | Set at | Purpose |                                                                                 
  184 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
  185 +| `size` | Constructor | Always `2`; used by renderer to draw the joined block |                                
  186 +| `this.col`, `this.row` | Constructor / doMove | Top-left corner of the current 2×2 footprint |                
  187 +                                                                                                                
  188 +#### Footprint                                                                                                  
  189 +                                                                                                                
  190 +At any time, Big Boy occupies:                                                                                  
  191 +```                                                                                                             
  192 +(col,   row),   (col+1, row)                                                                                    
  193 +(col,   row+1), (col+1, row+1)                                                                                  
  194 +```                                                                                                             
  195 +                                                                                                                
  196 +#### New Cell Calculation (`getNewCells(dc, dr)`)                                                               
  197 +                                                                                                                
  198 +```                                                                                                             
  199 +newCol = this.col + dc * 2                                                                                      
  200 +newRow = this.row + dr * 2                                                                                      
  201 +                                                                                                                
  202 +New footprint:                                                                                                  
  203 +(newCol,   newRow),   (newCol+1, newRow)                                                                        
  204 +(newCol,   newRow+1), (newCol+1, newRow+1)                                                                      
  205 +```                                                                                                             
  206 +                                                                                                                
  207 +Because `dc` and `dr` are either `-1`, `0`, or `+1` and the block is 2 wide/tall, multiplying by 2 places the ne
      +w footprint immediately adjacent to (not overlapping) the current footprint.                                    
  208 +                                                                                                                
  209 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  210 +                                                                                                                
  211 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
  212 +                                                                                                                
  213 +1. Start with direction array `[[0,-1],[0,1],[-1,0],[1,0]]` (up, down, left, right).                            
  214 +2. Fisher-Yates shuffle in-place.                                                                               
  215 +3. For each direction `[dc, dr]`:                                                                               
  216 +   - Compute the 4 destination cells via `getNewCells(dc, dr)`.                                                 
  217 +   - Call `canMoveTo` on all 4. If all pass: `doMove(dc, dr)`, return `true`.                                   
  218 +4. If no direction works: return `false` → **bot dies**.                                                        
  219 +                                                                                                                
  220 +#### `doMove(dc, dr)`                                                                                           
  221 +                                                                                                                
  222 +1. For each of the 4 new cells: call `collectPowerup` (in case a powerup is there), then set `game.cells[r][c] =
      + this`.                                                                                                         
  223 +2. Update `this.col += dc * 2` and `this.row += dr * 2`.                                                        
  224 +3. Old 4 cells are **not** cleared — they remain owned by Big Boy indefinitely.                                 
  225 +                                                                                                                
  226 +#### Scoring                                                                                                    
  227 +                                                                                                                
  228 +Each of the 4 cells in every footprint Big Boy has ever occupied counts as 1 point. A bot that has taken 10 move
      +s into new territory owns 40+ cells.                                                                            
  229 +                                                                                                                
  230 +#### Rendering Special Case                                                                                     
  231 +                                                                                                                
  232 +During the render scan, when a 2×2 block of cells all belong to the same bot instance with `size === 2`, a singl
      +e 18×18 rect is drawn instead of four separate 8×8 rects, and those four positions are skipped to avoid double-d
      +rawing.                                                                                                         
  233 +                                                                                                                
  234 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  235 +                                                                                                                
  236 +Dies when all four possible 2×2 destination footprints are blocked (contain at least one cell owned by a differe
      +nt bot or out of bounds).                                                                                       
  237 +                                                                                                                
  238 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
  239 +                                                                                                                
  240 +- **Speed Boost**: `ticksPerMove` drops to 5.                                                                   
  241 +- **Multiball**: spawns a new Big Boy at current position; it also occupies a 2×2 and moves independently.      
  242 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills this bot.                                                                         
  243 +                                                                                                                
  244  ---

  246  ### Hydra
   49 -**Color**: #aa44ff (purple) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1                                        
  247  
   51 -Moves like Chaos — random direction each turn. When completely blocked (all four cardinal directions are unavail
      -able), instead of dying normally, it **spawns two new Hydra bots** at its current position and then dies. The sp
      -awned children behave identically and can also split when blocked.                                              
  248 +**Class**: `HydraBot` | **File**: `js/bots/hydra.js`                                                            
  249 +**Color**: `#aa44ff` (purple) | **ticksPerMove**: 10 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 1 (grows)            
  250  
  251 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
  252 +                                                                                                                
  253 +Wanders randomly like Chaos. When completely blocked instead of dying, it splits into two children and then dies
      + itself.                                                                                                        
  254 +                                                                                                                
  255 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  256 +                                                                                                                
  257 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
  258 +                                                                                                                
  259 +1. Start with direction array `[[0,-1],[0,1],[-1,0],[1,0]]`.                                                    
  260 +2. Fisher-Yates shuffle in-place.                                                                               
  261 +3. For each direction: if `canMoveTo` passes, move there, return `true`.                                        
  262 +4. **If all four directions are blocked**:                                                                      
  263 +   - Call `game.spawnMidGame(HydraBot, this.col, this.row, this.color)` twice → two new Hydra bots appear at thi
      +s bot's current position.                                                                                       
  264 +   - Return `false` → this bot dies.                                                                            
  265 +                                                                                                                
  266 +#### Spawning Details                                                                                           
  267 +                                                                                                                
  268 +`spawnMidGame` creates a new `HydraBot` instance at `(col, row)` and pushes it into `game.bots`. Each child star
      +ts fresh with `moveCooldown = 0`, no teammates, no isLeader. Children behave identically and can also split when
      + blocked.                                                                                                       
  269 +                                                                                                                
  270 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  271 +                                                                                                                
  272 +The parent dies via `makeMove()` returning `false` after spawning children. Children die normally (all four neig
      +hbors blocked, no more spawning unless they also get blocked — they do also spawn when blocked).                
  273 +                                                                                                                
  274 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
  275 +                                                                                                                
  276 +- **Speed Boost**: speeds up this Hydra instance. Children spawned afterward start with `ticksPerMove` from `def
      +.ticksPerMove` (default 10), not the boosted value, because `spawnMidGame` uses the BOT_DEFS value. Children spa
      +wned via **Multiball** inherit the collector's current `ticksPerMove`.                                          
  277 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills this instance only (no teammates array).                                          
  278 +                                                                                                                
  279 +#### Notes                                                                                                      
  280 +                                                                                                                
  281 +- Hydra children are not linked as teammates. No `teammates` array is maintained. Each child is fully independen
      +t.                                                                                                              
  282 +- A cluster can grow without bound if each generation finds room to split before being cornered.                
  283 +

  286  ### Scout
   56 -**Color**: #ff55cc (pink) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 30 | **Count**: 3 bots per team | **Size**: 1×1             
  287  
   58 -Spawns as a team of 3 bots at the same starting position. Each bot independently picks a random cardinal directi
      -on and moves in a straight line until blocked by a wall or a different color. When blocked, shuffles the remaini
      -ng three directions and picks the first valid one.                                                              
  288 +**Class**: `ScoutBot` | **File**: `js/bots/scout.js`                                                            
  289 +**Color**: `#ff55cc` (pink) | **ticksPerMove**: 30 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 3                      
  290  
   60 -Scouts treat cells owned by their own team (same color) as passable — they do not stop when entering teammate te
      -rritory, though this does not count as claiming new land for stagnation purposes.                               
  291 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
  292  
   62 -All three bots' cell counts are pooled into a single "Scout" score. If any scout collects the Speed Boost poweru
      -p, all three teammates receive the speed boost simultaneously.                                                  
  293 +Three bots spawn together and each independently charges in a straight line until blocked, then randomly picks a
      + new direction. Scouts treat their own team's cells as passable.                                                
  294  
  295 +#### State                                                                                                      
  296 +                                                                                                                
  297 +| Property | Set at | Purpose |                                                                                 
  298 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
  299 +| `dc`, `dr` | Constructor | Current direction vector |                                                         
  300 +| `teammates` | `spawnBots` group setup | Array of the other two Scout instances |                              
  301 +| `isLeader` | `spawnBots` | `true` for the first bot in the group |                                            
  302 +                                                                                                                
  303 +Initial direction is chosen randomly from `[[0,-1],[0,1],[-1,0],[1,0]]` (up, down, left, right) for each bot ind
      +ependently.                                                                                                     
  304 +                                                                                                                
  305 +#### Custom `canMoveTo(col, row)`                                                                               
  306 +                                                                                                                
  307 +Scout overrides the global `canMoveTo` with its own method:                                                     
  308 +                                                                                                                
  309 +```                                                                                                             
  310 +cell === null                                                                                                   
  311 +|| cell === this           (own instance)                                                                       
  312 +|| cell.color === this.color   (any teammate or multiball-spawned Scout)                                        
  313 +```                                                                                                             
  314 +                                                                                                                
  315 +Walls (out-of-bounds) still block. This allows Scouts to pass through territory owned by their own team.        
  316 +                                                                                                                
  317 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  318 +                                                                                                                
  319 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
  320 +                                                                                                                
  321 +1. Compute `nc = this.col + this.dc`, `nr = this.row + this.dr`.                                                
  322 +2. If `this.canMoveTo(nc, nr)` passes: move there, return `true`. Direction unchanged.                          
  323 +3. **Current direction is blocked**:                                                                            
  324 +   - Build `alts`: the other three cardinal directions (all four minus the current `[this.dc, this.dr]`).       
  325 +   - Fisher-Yates shuffle `alts`.                                                                               
  326 +   - For each alt direction `[dc, dr]`:                                                                         
  327 +     - If `this.canMoveTo(this.col + dc, this.row + dr)` passes: update `this.dc = dc`, `this.dr = dr`, move the
      +re, return `true`.                                                                                              
  328 +4. If no direction works: return `false` → **this Scout dies**. Other team members continue independently.      
  329 +                                                                                                                
  330 +#### Scoring                                                                                                    
  331 +                                                                                                                
  332 +All three bots' owned cells are pooled under the "Scout" type (same `defIndex`). Moving through teammate cells d
      +oes not re-claim them — the cell remains owned by the original Scout.                                           
  333 +                                                                                                                
  334 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  335 +                                                                                                                
  336 +An individual Scout dies when all four cardinal neighbors are blocked (by walls or non-Scout-colored cells). Oth
      +er team members are unaffected.                                                                                 
  337 +                                                                                                                
  338 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
  339 +                                                                                                                
  340 +- **Speed Boost**: sets `ticksPerMove = 5` on the collecting bot AND all bots in its `teammates` array — all thr
      +ee Scouts speed up simultaneously.                                                                              
  341 +- **Multiball**: spawns a fourth Scout at the collecting bot's position. The new Scout is added to all existing 
      +Scouts' `teammates` arrays and receives all of them as its teammates. It picks its own random initial direction.
  342 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills the collecting Scout and all teammates — the entire three-bot team dies simultaneo
      +usly.                                                                                                           
  343 +                                                                                                                
  344  ---
  345  
  346  ### Bishop
   67 -**Color**: #00ccbb (teal) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Size**: 1×1                                          
  347  
   69 -Moves exclusively diagonally (never laterally or vertically). Picks a random diagonal direction at spawn — one o
      -f: up-left, up-right, down-left, down-right — and keeps moving in that direction until blocked by a wall or anot
      -her bot's color. When blocked, shuffles the other three diagonal directions and takes the first valid one. Dies 
      -if all four diagonals are blocked.                                                                              
  348 +**Class**: `BishopBot` | **File**: `js/bots/bishop.js`                                                          
  349 +**Color**: `#00ccbb` (teal) | **ticksPerMove**: 10 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 1                      
  350  
   71 -Due to diagonal-only movement, Bishop can only ever reach cells where `(col + row) % 2` matches its starting cel
      -l's parity — it covers at most half the grid.                                                                   
  351 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
  352  
  353 +Moves only diagonally. Charges in a chosen diagonal until blocked, then picks a new diagonal randomly.          
  354 +                                                                                                                
  355 +#### State                                                                                                      
  356 +                                                                                                                
  357 +| Property | Set at | Purpose |                                                                                 
  358 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
  359 +| `dc`, `dr` | Constructor | Current diagonal direction; both are always `+1` or `-1` |                         
  360 +                                                                                                                
  361 +Initial direction chosen randomly from `[[1,1],[1,-1],[-1,1],[-1,-1]]`.                                         
  362 +                                                                                                                
  363 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  364 +                                                                                                                
  365 +Each tick:                                                                                                      
  366 +                                                                                                                
  367 +1. Compute `nc = this.col + this.dc`, `nr = this.row + this.dr`.                                                
  368 +2. If `game.canMoveTo(nc, nr, this)` passes: move there, return `true`. Direction unchanged.                    
  369 +3. **Current diagonal is blocked**:                                                                             
  370 +   - Build `alts`: the other three diagonals (all four minus current).                                          
  371 +   - Fisher-Yates shuffle `alts`.                                                                               
  372 +   - For each alt `[dc, dr]`:                                                                                   
  373 +     - If `game.canMoveTo(this.col + dc, this.row + dr, this)` passes: update `this.dc = dc`, `this.dr = dr`, mo
      +ve there, return `true`.                                                                                        
  374 +4. If no diagonal works: return `false` → **bot dies**.                                                         
  375 +                                                                                                                
  376 +#### Parity Constraint                                                                                          
  377 +                                                                                                                
  378 +Because all moves change both `col` and `row` by ±1, the sum `col + row` alternates parity with every move. Bish
      +op can only ever occupy cells where `(col + row) % 2` matches its starting cell. It will permanently leave rough
      +ly half the grid unreachable.                                                                                   
  379 +                                                                                                                
  380 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  381 +                                                                                                                
  382 +Dies when all four diagonal neighbors are blocked (by walls, out-of-bounds, or cells owned by any other bot).   
  383 +                                                                                                                
  384 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                              
  385 +                                                                                                                
  386 +- **Speed Boost**: `ticksPerMove` drops to 5 — charges diagonals faster.                                        
  387 +- **Multiball**: spawns a second Bishop at current position with its own random initial diagonal.               
  388 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills this bot immediately.                                                             
  389 +                                                                                                                
  390  ---
  391  
  392  ### Drunk Jezzball
   76 -**Color**: #ff6644 (coral) | **Speed**: ticksPerMove 10 | **Count**: 2 bots per team | **Size**: 1×1            
  393  
   78 -Spawns as a pair at the same starting position. One bot is designated the **leader**.                           
  394 +**Class**: `DrunkJezzballBot` | **File**: `js/bots/drunk-jezzball.js`                                           
  395 +**Color**: `#ff6644` (coral) | **ticksPerMove**: 20 | **Size**: 1×1 | **Count per team**: 2                     
  396  
   80 -On spawn (and after each "stop"), the leader picks a random **axis** from four options:                         
   81 -- Left / Right (lateral)                                                                                        
   82 -- Up / Down (vertical)                                                                                          
   83 -- Up-left / Down-right (diagonal A)                                                                             
   84 -- Up-right / Down-left (diagonal B)                                                                             
  397 +#### Behavior                                                                                                   
  398  
   86 -The leader and its partner are assigned **opposite directions** along the chosen axis and immediately begin movi
      -ng away from each other.                                                                                        
  399 +Two bots launch in opposite directions along a shared axis. When both are stopped, the leader picks a new axis a
      +nd they launch again. The motion resembles a Jezzball line being drawn across the board.                        
  400  
   88 -Each bot independently moves one step per tick in its assigned direction. When a bot hits a wall or another colo
      -r, it sets itself as **stuck** and waits. When **both** bots are stuck, the leader picks a new axis and they set
      - off again.                                                                                                     
  401 +#### State                                                                                                      
  402  
   90 -If a bot is stuck and waiting, its stagnation counter increments each tick — if stuck for 100 consecutive ticks,
      - it dies. If one bot dies, the other continues briefly on its own until it stagnates.                           
  403 +| Property | Set at | Purpose |                                                                                 
  404 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
  405 +| `isLeader` | `spawnBots` | `true` for the first bot in the pair |                                             
  406 +| `teammates` | `spawnBots` | Array of length 1 containing the other bot |                                      
  407 +| `dc`, `dr` | `chooseNewAxis` | Current direction vector (set before first move) |                             
  408 +| `stuck` | Constructor / `makeMove` | `true` = bot is waiting; `false` = bot is actively moving |              
  409  
   92 -Speed Boost on either bot propagates to the partner.                                                            
  410 +`get partner()` returns `this.teammates[0]` — a convenience alias.                                              
  411 +                                                                                                                
  412 +#### Axes                                                                                                       
  413 +                                                                                                                
  414 +`chooseNewAxis()` picks randomly from four axis pairs:                                                          
  415 +                                                                                                                
  416 +| Axis | Direction A | Direction B |                                                                            
  417 +|---|---|---|                                                                                                   
  418 +| Lateral | `[-1, 0]` (left) | `[1, 0]` (right) |                                                               
  419 +| Vertical | `[0, -1]` (up) | `[0, 1]` (down) |                                                                 
  420 +| Diagonal A | `[-1, -1]` (up-left) | `[1, 1]` (down-right) |                                                   
  421 +| Diagonal B | `[-1, 1]` (down-left) | `[1, -1]` (up-right) |                                                   
  422 +                                                                                                                
  423 +One direction is assigned to the leader and the opposite to the partner (randomly swapped so either can go eithe
      +r way).                                                                                                         
  424 +                                                                                                                
  425 +Both bots have `stuck` set to `false` after axis selection.                                                     
  426 +                                                                                                                
  427 +#### Initialization                                                                                             
  428 +                                                                                                                
  429 +`onGroupReady()` is called on the leader immediately after the group is linked by `spawnBots`. It calls `chooseN
      +ewAxis()`, which sets both bots' directions and clears both `stuck` flags. This happens before the first tick.  
  430 +                                                                                                                
  431 +#### Movement Algorithm                                                                                         
  432 +                                                                                                                
  433 +Each tick (for each bot independently):                                                                         
  434 +                                                                                                                
  435 +1. **If not stuck**:                                                                                            
  436 +   - Compute `nc = this.col + this.dc`, `nr = this.row + this.dr`.                                              
  437 +   - If `canMoveTo(nc, nr, this)` passes: move there, return `true`.                                            
  438 +   - Otherwise: set `this.stuck = true` (fall through to stuck logic).                                          
  439 +2. **If stuck (including just-set)**:                                                                           
  440 +   - If this bot `isLeader` AND `this.partner` exists AND `this.partner.stuck`:                                 
  441 +     - Both bots are stopped → call `chooseNewAxis()` (a new axis is picked, both `stuck` cleared, new direction
      +s assigned).                                                                                                    
  442 +   - Otherwise: increment `this.movesSinceNewLand++` (waiting for partner).                                     
  443 +   - Return `true` (stuck bots do not die from returning false — they always return `true`).                    
  444 +                                                                                                                
  445 +#### Death Condition                                                                                            
  446 +                                                                                                                
  447 +`makeMove()` always returns `true`, so Drunk Jezzball bots **never die from movement failure**. They wait indefi
      439 +2. **If stuck (including just-set)**:                                                                       
      440 +   - If this bot `isLeader` AND `this.partner` exists AND `this.partner.stuck`:                             
      441 +     - Both bots are stopped → call `chooseNewAxis()` (a new axis is picked, both `stuck` cleared, new      
          + directions assigned).                                                                                      
      442 +   - Otherwise: increment `this.movesSinceNewLand++` (waiting for partner).                                 
      443 +   - Return `true` (stuck bots do not die from returning false — they always return `true`).                
      444 +                                                                                                            
      445 +#### Death Condition                                                                                        
      446 +                                                                                                            
      447 +`makeMove()` always returns `true`, so Drunk Jezzball bots **never die from movement failure**. They w      
          +ait indefinitely until conditions change. The game ends from the timer or all-bots-dead (which cannot       
          +happen for Drunk Jezzball from movement alone).                                                             
      448 +                                                                                                            
      449 +If one bot's `partner` is null (e.g., the partner died from an instant death!!! powerup), the survivin      
          +g bot becomes stuck permanently: it hits a wall, sets `stuck = true`, then each tick checks `partner.s      
          +tuck` — but `partner` is null, so the condition `this.partner && this.partner.stuck` is false. The bot      
          + loops incrementing `movesSinceNewLand` forever.                                                            
      450 +                                                                                                            
      451 +#### Powerup Notes                                                                                          
      452 +                                                                                                            
      453 +- **Speed Boost**: sets `ticksPerMove = 5` on the collecting bot and its partner simultaneously.            
      454 +- **Multiball**: spawns a third Drunk Jezzball at current position; the new bot joins the teammates ar      
          +rays. With three bots, the leader's "both stuck" check (`this.partner.stuck`) only examines the first        
          +teammate — the third bot is linked but the axis-change trigger is only a two-bot check.               
      455 +- **Instant death!!!**: kills the collecting bot and its partner — entire team dies.                  
      456 +                                                                                                      
      457 +#### Notes                                                                                            
      458 +                                                                                                      
      459 +- The axis-selection check only examines `this.partner` (i.e., `this.teammates[0]`). A Multiball-spawn
          +ed third bot has no special role in triggering re-launch.                                             
      460 +- Both bots move independently on each tick. There is no synchronization — one bot may have already mo
          +ved multiple cells while the other is still approaching its wall, since they tick separately.

● All done. Here's what was added:                                                                                      
                                                                                                                        
  - "He's on Fire!!" powerup: sets onFire = true on the collecting bot and all teammates. Lasts the rest of the game.   
  - Invulnerability: game.canMoveTo and ScoutBot.canMoveTo both return true for any in-bounds cell when bot.onFire, so  
  fire bots can move into and claim any enemy territory.                                                                
  - Fire outline: drawBot uses sin(Date.now() / 150) to cycle t between 0 and 1, mapping to rgb(255, 0→255, 0→255) — red
   at the low end, orange at the midpoint, white at the peak — all at 60fps since render() is called every tick.        
  - Icon: 🔥 appears in the settings panel and on the leaderboard when collected.
